If you want to rebuttal, do it. Why is Dicatorship fasist?
Dictatorship can adopt fascist characteristics due to its inherent concentration of power in the hands of a single individual or a small group, often coupled with authoritarian control and suppression of dissent. Fascism, as a specific political ideology, thrives on authoritarianism, nationalism, and totalitarianism. In a dictatorship, these traits can manifest in the form of strict government control over all aspects of society, promotion of a strong nationalistic identity, and the use of propaganda to manipulate public opinion.
Furthermore, dictatorships may employ tactics commonly associated with fascism, such as censorship, persecution of minorities or political opponents, and the glorification of militarism. By fostering a cult of personality around the leader and emphasizing the supremacy of the state, dictators with fascist inclinations seek to maintain power through fear, coercion, and the suppression of individual freedoms.
While not all dictatorships are inherently fascist, the potential for dictatorship to evolve into a fascist regime arises from the unchecked concentration of power and the erosion of democratic institutions. Thus, the fusion of dictatorship with fascist ideology can pose a grave threat to liberty, human rights, and the principles of democracy.

Guys sun drop is writing what the words mean
Done?
Narcissistic: Narcissistic personality disorder is a mental health condition in which people have an unreasonably high sense of their own importance. They need and seek too much attention and want people to admire them. People with this disorder may lack the ability to understand or care about the feelings of others.
Antisocial: Antisocial personality disorder, sometimes called sociopathy, is a mental health condition in which a person consistently shows no regard for right and wrong and ignores the rights and feelings of others
Histrionic: a type of psychiatric disorder that features attention-seeking behaviours, seductive behaviour and emotional over-reaction
Dependent:  It causes feelings of helplessness, submissiveness, a need to be taken care of and for constant reassurance, and an inability to make everyday decisions without an excessive amount of advice and reassurance from others
Sadistic: Someone who gets pleasure from hurting or humiliating others is a sadist
Compulsive: Obsessive-compulsive personality disorder is characterized by a pervasive preoccupation with orderliness, perfectionism, and control (with no room for flexibility) that ultimately slows or interferes with completing a task
Negativistic: When you believe you dont deserve something/keep being negative
Avoidant: excessive social anxiety and inhibition, fear of intimacy (despite an intense desire for it), severe feelings of inadequacy and inferiority, and an overreliance on avoidance of feared stimuli
Depressive: You know right?
Masochistic: deriving pleasure or sexual gratification from being abused or dominated
Borderline: Borderline personality disorder is a mental health condition that affects the way people feel about themselves and others, making it hard to function in everyday life. It includes a pattern of unstable, intense relationships, as well as impulsiveness and an unhealthy way of seeing themselves. Impulsiveness involves having extreme emotions and acting or doing things without thinking about them first.
Paranoid: a person has a long-term pattern of distrust and suspicion of others
Schzoid: a condition where a person shows very little, if any, interest and ability to form relationships with other people
Schizotypal: is a mental health condition marked by a consistent pattern of intense discomfort with relationships and social interactions
Hypomaniac: a condition in which you have a period of abnormally elevated, extreme changes in your mood or emotions, energy level or activity level

from math import floor
import sys
N = 69420
N += 1 # it gives a null digit let's just ignore that
N += 1 # This one makes sense, most people don't count the 3 but the program does
len = floor(10*N/3)+1
A = [2] * len
nines = 0
predigit = 0
for j in range(1,N+1):
    q = 0
    for i in range(len,0,-1):
        x = 10*A[i-1] + q*i
        A[i-1] = x % (2*i - 1)
        q = x // (2*i - 1)
    A[0] = q%10
    q = q//10
    if(q == 9):
        nines += 1
    elif(q == 10):
        if(j!=1):print(predigit+1,end="",flush=True)
        for k in range(nines):
            if(j!=1):print("0",end="",flush=True)
        predigit, nines = 0,0
    else:
        if(j!=1):print(predigit,end="",flush=True)
        predigit = q
        for k in range(nines):
            if(j!=1):print("9",end="",flush=True)
        nines = 0
print(predigit)
